Mosaic release: v7

Mirrored from https://s3.amazonaws.com/grizli-v2/JwstMosaics/v7/index.html .

What's new?

July 2023

  • Mosaics created with the new jwst weighting strategy to address the issues described here and here
  • Catalogs and photometric redshifts in prep (14 July 2023)
  • Abell 2744
    • Expanded mosaic footprint to include all available JWST data
    • Mosaics include data from GLASS obtained July 2023
  • GOODS-North (gdn)
    • Includes a few pointings from the PANORAMIC (GO-2514) pure parallel program
  • GOODS-South (gds)
    • Includes all public imaging data from the FRESCO (GO-1895), JEMS (GO-1963) and JADES (GTO-1210) programs.
  • PRIMER (primer-uds, primer-cosmos)
    • COSMOS cosaic expanded w.r.t. v6 to encompass the full PRIMER NIRCam + MIRI mosaic, now including both epochs/orientations.
    • The mosaics in both PRIMER fields are huge! NIRCam SW mosaics in both PRIMER fields are created with the same 40 mas pixel grid as LW.
    • Updated HST mosaics included here on the new COSMOS pixel grid. UDS is unchanged from v6.
    • Some improvement in the PRIMER MIRI reductions using time-dependent sky flats.

14 August 2023

  • PRIMER August 2023 (primer-uds, primer-cosmos)
    • Mosaics in both fields split in half, with overlaps, to facilitate catalog generation. Both halves created with a common tangent point.
      primer-cosmos-east / west

      primer-uds-north / south
    • All mosaics still have 40mas pixels, both SW and LW
    • HST mosaics created on the updated pixel grids
    • UDS includes the most recent visits from August 2023
    • All JWST PRIMER-UDS have been fully reprocessed with the following modifications
      • Individual Level1 NIRCam exposures reprocessed with improved treatment of the snowballs ( grizli.jwst_level1)
      • All PRIMER visits aligned to a new full astrometric catalog generated from the F444W mosaic, which itself was aligned to the HSC ultra-deep i-band catalog.
  • Added mosaics of the elgordo field ( ACT CLJ0102-49151, GTO-1176)
